 input- IANS In case of insolvency of the company, the matter goes to NCLT, after which an Insolvency Professional is appointed
 National Company Law Appellate Tribunal National Company Law Appellate Tribunal (NCLAT) was constituted under Section 410 of the Companies Act 2013
 ye 1 june 2016 se rashtriya company kanoon nyaayaadhikaran (ensielti) ke adeshon ke khilaaf apil kii sunwaayee ke liye banaaya gaya tribunel he
 Explain that the case first goes to the National Company Law Tribunal (NCLT) on the insolvency of a company
 yahaan iske liye inasolvency profeshnal niyukt kiya jaataa he, jise yah jimmaa saunpa jaataa he ki wo 180 dinon ke bheetar company ko rivive karne kaa prayaas kare
 If the company is revived within 180 days, then it starts functioning again
 agar aisa nahin hota to use diwalia maanakar aage kii karrwai kii jaati he
 The NCLAT has been acting as an Appellate Tribunal for hearing appeals against orders given by the NCLT under Section 61 of the Insolvency and Bankruptcy Code 2016 (IBC) with effect from December 1, 2016
 NCLAT sunwaayee kii apil ke liye apiliy nyaayaadhikaran bhi he
 It works against orders passed by the Insolvency and Bankruptcy Board of India under Section 202 and Section 211 of the IBC
 NCLAT company ke adhinium 2013 kii dhara 410 main laae gaye sanshodhan ke anusaar bharat ke pratispardhaa ayog (CCI) dwaara jari kiye gaye kisi bhi disha-nirdesh yaa nirnay ko paarit karne yaa kiye gaye aadesh ke khilaaf apil ko sunne or nipataane ke liye apiliy nyaayaadhikaran bhi he
 According to Section 172 of 2013, the Finance Act, 2017 will be effective from 26 May 2017
 nyaayamurti es
 J
 supreme court ke purv nyaayadhish mukhopadhyaay ab NCLAT ke adhyaksh hai

 The report said that there were clear indications that some groups and self-appointed or self-appointed clergy had converted from seven districts of Kolar, Bangalore, Chikkaballapur, Bellary, Davanagre, Chikmagalur and Udupi using unaccounted local or foreign funds

 sitambar 2008 main mangalore, udupi, chikmagalore, kolar, chikballarpur, bellari or daavangere jilon main girjagharon par hamale kiye gaye the
 The report said that the attacks were carried out by known or unknown organizations and misled against Christianity or Christianity by radical naughty elements who misunderstood that they would be protected by the ruling party
 ayog ne yah bhi sifarish kii ki vah dharm ke naam par kisi bhi vyakti par atyaachaar rokna or sabko suraksha dena sunishchit kare
 The commission, which considered over a thousand petitions and cross-examined 800 witnesses in a two-year investigation, said that some incidents of the attack were true, some were fabricated, some were exaggerated and some were purely politically motivated
 report main haalanki dakshin kannada main kuch carch parisaron main kanoonee jaruraton kaa anupaalan kiye bagaiyr police ke pravesh ko avivekpurna asangat or anubhavheen kadam qaraar diya gaya or kaha gaya ki yah samvidhan ke tahat sangrakshit dharmik hiton tathaa maanavadhikaron kaa ulanghan he

 report main peediton tathaa charchon ko paryaapt muaavja die jane kaa paksh liya gaya or kaha gaya ki abhi di gai muaavja raashi kam he
 The Commission said that it is true that some people involved in the conversion are getting funds from some sources including abroad and they are misusing this money in mass conversions of innocent and helpless people belonging to weaker sections of society
 is sambandh main ayog ne padariyon kii gatividhiyon ke byore or aavashyak vittiya jaanch kaa paksh liya
